     hatv/Aya /S/atrUn v/i bhajasva v/eda /ojo m/imAno v/i m/rdho nudasva //2//

|p1  t/ad /id Asa bh/uvaneSu jy/eSTham y/ato yaj~N/a ugr/as tveS/an.rmNaH /

     svad/oH sv/AdIyaH svAd/unA s.rjA s/am ad/aH s/u m/adhu m/adhunAbh/i yodhIH //3//

|p1  sAhasr/as tveS/a .rSabh/aH p/ayasvAn v/i/SvA rUp/ANi vakS/aNAsu b/ibhrat /
     bhadr/aM dAtr/e y/ajamAnAya /SIkSan bArhaspaty/a usr/iyas t/antum /AtAn //1//
|p2  ap/AM y/o /agne pratim/A babh/Uva prabh/UH s/arvasmai p.rthiv/Iva dev/I /
     pit/A vats/AnAM p/atir aghny/AnAM sAhasr/e p/oSe /api naH k.rNotu //2//
|p3  p/umAn ant/arvAn tsth/aviraH p/ayasvAn v/asoH k/abandhaM .rSabh/o bibharti /
     t/am /indrAya path/ibhir devay/Anair hut/am agn/ir vahatu jAt/avedAH //3//
|p4  pit/A vats/AnAM p/atir aghny/AnAM /atho pit/A mahat/AM g/argarANAm /
     vats/o jar/Ayu pratidh/uk pIy/USa Am/ikSA gh.rt/aM t/ad v asya r/etaH //4//
|p5  dev/AnAM bhAg/a upanAh/a eS/o 'p/AM r/asa /oSadhInAM gh.rt/asya /
     s/omasya bhakS/am av.rNIta /Sakr/o b.rh/ann /adrir abhavad y/ac ch/arIram //5//
|p6  s/omena pUrN/aM kal/a/SaM bibharSi tv/astA rup/ANAM janit/A pa/SUn/Am /

|p7  /AjaM bibharti gh.rt/am asya r/etaH sAhasr/aH p/oSas t/am u yaj~N/am AhuH /
     /indrasya rUp/am .rSabh/o v/asAnaH s/o asm/An devAH /Siv/a a/itu datt/aH //7//
|p8  /indrasya/ujo v/aruNasya bAh/U a/Sv/inor /aMsau mar/utAm iy/aM kak/ut /
     b/rhasp/atiM s/aMbh.rtam et/am Ahur y/e dh/IrAsaH kav/ayo y/e manIS/iNaH //8//
|p9  da/ivIr v/i/SaH p/ayasvAn /A tanoSi tv/Am /indraM tv/AM s/arasvantam AhuH /
     sah/asraM s/a /ekamukhA dadAti y/o brAhmaN/a .rSabh/am Ajuh/oti //9//
|p10  b/rhasp/atiH savit/A te v/ayo dadhau tv/aSTur vAy/oH p/ary Atm/A ta /Abh.rtaH /

     aSThIv/antAv abravIn mitr/o m/amaita/u k/evalAv /iti //12//

     p/ucchaM v/Atasya dev/asya t/ena dhUnoty /oSadhIH //13//

|p15  kroD/a AsIj jAmi/SaMs/asya s/omasya kl/a/So dh.rt/aH /
     dev/AH saMg/atya y/at s/arva .rSabh/aM vy/akalpayan //15//

|p18  /Satay/AjaM s/a yajate na/inaM dunvanty agn/ayaH /

|p19  brAhmaN/ebhya .rSabh/aM dattv/A v/arIyaH k.rNute m/anaH /

|p1  /indrasya pratham/o r/atho dev/AnAm /aparo r/atho v/aruNasya t.rt/Iya /it /

     paidv/o ratharvy/AH /S/iraH s/aM bibheda p.rdAkv/AH //5//
|p6  pa/idva pr/ehi pratham/o 'nu tvA vay/am /emasi /
     /ahIn vy \asyatAt path/o y/ena smA vay/am em/asi //6//
|p7  id/aM paidv/o ajAyated/am asya par/AyaNam /
     im/Any /arvataH pad/Ahighny/o vAj/inIvataH //7//
|p8  s/aMyataM n/a v/i Sparad vy/AttaM n/a s/aM yamat /

     s/a ebhyo j/itim /id duhe bh/UyobhUyaH /Sv/aH/Svas t/ena tv/aM dviSat/o jahi //16//

     t/am im/aM dev/atA maN/iM pr/aty amu~Ncanta /Sambh/uvam /
     s/a Abhyo v/i/Svam /id duhe bh/UyobhUyaH /Sv/aH/Svas t/ena tv/aM dviSat/o jahi //17//

|p1  y/o bhUt/aM ca bh/avyaM ca s/arvaM y/a/S cAdhit/iSThati /

     y/a /Ahutim aty/amanyanta dev/A ap/AM net/AraH katam/e t/a Asan //35//
|p36  im/Am eSAM p.rthiv/IM v/asta /eko 'nt/arikSaM p/ary /eko babhUva /

     t/AbhyAm enaM pr/A/SiSaM t/AbhyAm enam ajIgamam /
     eS/a v/A odan/aH s/arvA.NgaH s/arvaparuH s/arvatanUH /
     s/arvA.Nga ev/a s/arvaparuH s/arvatanUH s/aM bhavati y/a ev/aM v/eda //16//
|p48 {17}  t/ata/S cainam any/AbhyAm h/astAbhyAM pr/A/SIr y/AbhyAM cait/am p/Urva /rSayaH pr/A/Snan /
     brAhmaN/aM haniSyas/Ity enam Aha /
     t/aM v/A ah/aM nArv/A~NcaM n/a p/arA~NcaM n/a praty/a~Ncam /
     .rt/asya h/astAbhyAm /
     t/AbhyAm enam pr/A/SiSaM t/AbhyAm enam ajIgamam /
     eS/a v/A odan/aH s/arvA.NgaH s/arvaparuH s/arvatanUH /
     s/arvA.Nga ev/a s/arvaparuH s/arvatanUH s/aM bhavati y/a ev/aM v/eda //17//
|p49 {18}  t/ata/S cainam any/ayA pratiSTh/ayA pr/A/SIr y/ayA cait/aM p/Urva /rSayaH pr/A/Snan /
     apratiSThAn/o 'nAyatan/o mariSyas/Ity enam Aha /
     t/aM v/A ah/aM nArv/A~NcaM n/a p/arA~NcaM n/a praty/a~Ncam /
     saty/e pratiSTh/Aya /
     t/ayainaM pr/A/SiSaM t/ayainam ajIgamam /
     eS/a v/A odan/aH s/arvA.NgaH s/arvaparuH s/arvatanUH /
     s/arvA.Nga ev/a s/arvaparuH s/arvatanUH s/aM bhavati y/a ev/aM v/eda //18//
{5}
|p50 {1}  et/ad va/i bradhn/asya viST/apaM y/ad odan/aH //1//

|p1  prAN/Aya n/amo y/asya s/arvam id/aM v/a/Se /

     n/amas te prANa vidy/ute n/amas te prANa v/arSate //2//

|c1
|p1  saty/aM b.rh/ad .rt/am ugr/aM dIkS/A t/apo br/ahma yaj~N/aH p.rthiv/IM dhArayanti /
     s/A no bhUt/asya bh/avyasya p/atny ur/uM lok/aM p.rthiv/I naH k.rNotu  //1//
|p2  asaMbAdh/aM madhyat/o mAnav/AnAM y/asyA udv/ataH prav/ataH sam/aM bah/u /
     n/AnAvIryA /oSadhIr y/A b/ibharti p.rthiv/I naH prathatAM r/AdhyatAM naH  //2//
|p3  y/asyAM samudr/a ut/a s/indhur /Apo y/asyAm /annaM k.rST/ayaH saMbabhUv/uH  /
     y/asyAm id/aM j/invati prAN/ad /ejat s/A no bh/UmiH pUrvap/eye dadhAtu  //3//
|p4  y/asyA/S c/atasraH prad/i/SaH p.rthivy/A y/asyAm /annam k.rST/ayaH saMbabhUv/uH  /
     y/A b/ibharti bahudh/A prAN/ad /ejat s/A no bh/Umir g/oSv /apy /anne dadhAtu //4//
|p5  y/asyAM p/Urve pUrvajan/A vicakrir/e y/asyAM dev/A /asurAn abhy/avartayan  /
     g/avAm /a/SvAnAM v/ayasa/S ca viSTh/A bh/agaM v/arcaH p.rthiv/I no dadhAtu  //5//
|p6  vi/SvaMbhar/A vasudh/AnI pratiSTh/A h/iraNyavakSA j/agato niv/e/SanI /
     vai/SvAnar/aM b/ibhratI bh/Umir agn/im /indra.rSabhA dr/aviNe no dadhAtu //6//
|p7  y/AM r/akSanty asvapn/A vi/Svad/AnIM dev/A bh/UmiM p.rthiv/Im /apramAdam  /
     s/A no m/adhu priy/aM duhAm /atho ukSatu v/arcasA  //7//
|p8  y/ArNav/e 'dhi salil/am /agra /AsIt y/AM mAy/Abhir anv/acaran manIS/iNaH  /
     y/asyA h/rdayaM param/e vy\oman tsaty/en/Av.rtam am/rtaM p.rthivy/AH  /
     s/A no bh/Umis tv/iSiM b/alaM rASTr/e dadhAtUttam/e  //8//
|p9  y/asyAm /ApaH paricar/AH samAn/Ir ahorAtr/e /apramAdaM kS/aranti  /
     s/A no bh/Umir bh/UridhArA p/ayo duhAm /atho ukSatu v/arcasA  //9//
|p10  y/Am a/Sv/inAv /amimAtAM v/iSNur y/asyAM vicakram/e  /
     /indro y/AM cakr/a Atm/ane 'namitr/AM /S/acIp/atiH /
     s/A no bh/Umir v/i s.rjatAM mAt/A putr/Aya me p/ayaH  //10//
|p11  gir/ayas te p/arvatA him/avant/o 'raNyaM te p.rthivi syon/am astu  /
     babhr/uM k.rSN/Am r/ohiNIM vi/Sv/arUpAM dhruv/AM bh/UmiM p.rthiv/Im /indraguptAm  /
     /ajIt/o 'hato /akSat/o 'dhy aSThAm p.rthiv/Im /aham  //11//
|p12  y/at te m/adhyaM p.rthivi y/ac ca n/abhyaM y/As ta /Urjas tanv\aH saMbabhUv/uH  /
     t/Asu no dhehy abh/i naH pavasva mAt/A bh/UmiH putr/o ah/aM p.rthivy/AH parj/anyaH pit/A s/a u naH pipartu  //12//
|p13  y/asyAM v/ediM parig.rhN/anti bh/UmyAM y/asyAM yaj~N/aM tanv/ate vi/Sv/akarmANaH  /
     y/asyAM mIy/ante sv/aravaH p.rthivy/Am Urdhv/AH /Sukr/A /AhutyAH pur/astAt  /
     s/A no bh/Umir vardhayad v/ardhamAnA  //13//
|p14  y/o no dv/eSat p.rthivi y/aH p.rtany/Ad y/o 'bhid/AsAn m/anasA y/o vadh/ena  /
     t/aM no bhUme randhaya pUrvak.rtvari  //14//
|p15  tv/aj jAt/As tv/ayi caranti m/artyAs tv/aM bibharSi dvip/adas tv/aM c/atuSpadaH  /
     t/avem/e p.rthivi p/a~Nca mAnav/A y/ebhyo jy/otir am/rtaM m/artyebhya udy/an ts/Uryo ra/Sm/ibhir Atan/oti  //15//
|p16  t/A naH praj/AH s/aM duhratAM samagr/A vAc/o m/adhu p.rthivi dhehi m/ahyam  //16//
|p17  vi/Svasv\aM mAt/aram /oSadhInAM dhruv/AM bh/UmiM p.rthiv/IM dh/armaNA dh.rt/Am  /
     /Siv/AM syon/Am /anu carema vi/Sv/ahA  //17//
|p18  mah/at sadh/asthaM mahat/I babh/Uvitha mah/An v/ega ej/athur vep/athuS Te  /
     mah/AMs tv/endro rakSaty /apramAdam  /
     s/A no bhUme pr/a rocaya h/iraNyasyeva saMd/r/Si m/A no dvikSata k/a/S can/a  //18//
|p19  agn/ir bh/UmyAm /oSadhISv agn/im /Apo bibhraty agn/ir /a/Smasu  /
     agn/ir ant/aH p/uruSeSu g/oSv /a/SveSv agn/ayaH  //19//
|p20  agn/ir div/a /A tapaty agn/er dev/asyorv \a1nt/arikSam  /
     agn/iM m/artAsa indhate havyav/AhaM gh.rtapr/iyam  //20//
|p21  agn/ivAsAH p.rthivy \asitaj~N/Us tv/iSImantaM s/aM/SitaM mA k.rNotu  //21//
|p22  bh/UmyAM dev/ebhyo dadati yaj~N/aM havy/am /araMk.rtam /
     bh/UmyAM manuSy\A jIvanti svadh/ay/Annena m/artyAH /
     s/A no bh/UmiH prAN/am /Ayur dadhAtu jar/adaSTiM mA p.rthiv/I k.rNotu  //22//
|p23  y/as te gandh/aH p.rthivi saMbabh/Uva y/aM b/ibhraty /oSadhayo y/am /ApaH /
     y/aM gandharv/A apsar/asa/S ca bhejir/e t/ena mA surabh/iM k.rNu m/A no dvikSata k/a/S can/a  //23//
|p24  y/as te gandh/aH p/uSkaram Aviv/e/Sa y/aM saMjabhr/uH sUry/AyA vivAh/e /
     /amartyAH p.rthivi gandh/am /agre t/ena m/A surabh/iM k.rNu m/A no dvikSata k/a/S can/a  //24//
|p25  y/as te gandh/aH p/uruSeSu strIS/u puMs/u bh/ago r/uciH /
     y/o /a/SveSu vIr/eSu y/o m.rg/eSUt/a hast/iSu /
     kany\AyAM v/arco y/ad bhUme t/enAsm/A~M /api s/aM s.rja m/A no dvikSata k/a/S can/a  //25//
|p26  /Sil/A bh/Umir /a/SmA pAMs/uH s/A bh/UmiH s/aMdh.rtA dh.rt/A /
     t/asyai h/iraNyavakSase p.rthivy/A akaraM n/amaH  //26//
|p27  y/asyAM v.rkS/A vAnaspaty/A dhruv/As t/iSThanti vi/Sv/ahA /
     p.rthiv/IM vi/Sv/adhAyasaM dh.rt/Am acch/AvadAmasi  //27//
|p28  ud/IrANA ut/AsInAs t/iSThantaH prakr/AmantaH /
     padbhy/AM dakSiNasavy/AbhyAM m/A vyathiSmahi bh/UmyAm  //28//
|p29  vim/rgvarIM p.rthiv/Im /A vadAmi kSam/AM bh/UmiM br/ahmaNA vAv.rdhAn/Am /
     /UrjaM puST/aM b/ibhratIm annabhAg/aM gh.rt/aM tvAbhi n/i SIdema bhUme  //29//

|p31  y/As te pr/AcIH prad/i/So y/A /udIcIr y/As te bhUme adhar/Ad y/A/S ca pa/Sc/At  /

     t/Avan me c/akSur m/A meST/ottarAmuttarAM s/amAm  //33//
|p34  y/ac ch/ayAnaH pary/Avarte d/akSiNaM sakhy/am abh/i bhUme pAr/Sv/am uttAn/As tvA prat/IcIM y/at p.rST/Ibhir adhi/S/emahe /
     m/A hiMsIs t/atra no bhUme s/arvasya prati/SIvari  //34//

|p36  grISm/as te bhUme varS/ANi /Sar/ad dhemant/aH /S/i/Siro vasant/aH  /

     p/arA d/asyUn d/adatI devapIy/Un /indraM v.rNAn/A p.rthiv/I n/a v.rtr/am /Sakr/Aya dadhre v.rSabh/Aya v/rSNe  //37//
|p38  y/asyAM sadohavirdhAn/e y/Upo y/asyAM nimIy/ate /
     brahm/ANo y/asyAm /arcanty .rgbh/iH s/AmnA yajurv/idaH yujy/ante y/asyAm .rtv/ijaH s/omam /indrAya p/Atave  //38//
|p39  y/asyAM p/Urve bhUtak/rta /rSayo g/A /udAn.rc/uH /

     bh/ago anupr/ayu.NktAm /indra etu purogav/aH  //40//
|p41  y/asyAM g/Ayanti n/rtyanti bh/UmyAM m/artyA vya\ilabAH /
     yudhy/ante y/asyAm Akrand/o y/asyAm v/adati dundubh/iH /
     s/A no bh/UmiH pr/a NudatAM sap/atnAn asapatn/aM mA p.rthiv/I k.rNotu  //41//

|p43  y/asyAH p/uro dev/ak.rtAH kS/etre y/asyA vikurv/ate /
     praj/ApatiH p.rthiv/IM vi/Sv/agarbhAm /A/SAmA/SAM r/aNyAM naH k.rNotu  //43//

     ya/iH saMc/aranty ubh/aye bhadrapAp/As t/aM p/anthAnaM jayemAnamitr/am ataskar/aM y/ac chiv/aM t/ena no m.rDa  //47//
|p48  malv/aM b/ibhratI gurubh/rd bhadrapAp/asya nidh/anaM titikS/uH /
     varAh/eNa p.rthiv/I saMvidAn/A sUkar/Aya v/i jihIte m.rg/Aya  //48//
|p49  y/e ta AraNy/AH pa/S/avo m.rg/A v/ane hit/AH siMh/A vyAghr/AH puruS/Ada/S c/aranti  /
     ul/aM v/rkaM p.rthivi ducch/unAm it/a .rkS/IkAM r/akSo /apa bAdhayAsm/at  //49//

     pi/SAc/An ts/arvA r/akSAMsi t/An asm/ad bhUme yAvaya  //50//
|p51  y/AM dvip/AdaH pakS/iNaH saMp/atanti haMs/AH suparN/AH /Sakun/A v/ayAMsi  /
     y/asyAM v/Ato mAtar/i/Sv/eyate r/ajAMsi k.rNv/aM/S cyAv/ayaM/S ca v.rkS/An /
     v/Atasya prav/Am upav/Am /anu vAty arc/iH  //51//
|p52  y/asyAM k.rSN/am aruN/aM ca s/aMhite ahorAtr/e v/ihite bh/UmyAm /adhi /
     varS/eNa bh/UmiH p.rthiv/I v.rt/Av.rtA s/A no dadhAtu bhadr/ayA priy/e dh/AmanidhAmani  //52//
|p53  dya/u/S ca ma id/aM p.rthiv/I cAnt/arikSaM ca me vy/acaH /
     agn/iH s/Urya /Apo medh/AM v/i/Sve dev/A/S ca s/aM daduH  //53//
|p54  ah/am asmi s/ahamAna /uttaro n/Ama bh/UmyAm /
     abhIS/AD asmi vi/SvAS/AD /A/SAmA/SAM viSAsah/iH  //54//
|p55  ad/o y/ad devi pr/athamAnA pur/astAd deva/ir ukt/A vy/asarpo mahitv/am /
     /A tvA subhUt/am avi/Sat tad/AnIm /akalpayathAH prad/i/Sa/S c/atasraH  //55//
|p56  y/e gr/AmA y/ad /araNyaM y/AH sabh/A /adhi bh/UmyAm /
     y/e saMgrAm/AH s/amitayas t/eSu c/Aru vadema te  //56//
|p57  /a/Sva iva r/ajo dudhuve v/i t/An j/anAn y/a /AkSiyan p.rthiv/IM y/Ad /ajAyata /

|p58  y/ad v/adAmi m/adhumat t/ad vadAmi y/ad /IkSe t/ad vananti mA /
     tv/iSImAn asmi jUtim/An /avAny/An hanmi d/odhataH  //58//
|p59  /Santiv/A surabh/iH syon/A kIl/AlodhnI p/ayasvatI /
     bh/Umir /adhi bravItu me p.rthiv/I p/ayasA sah/a //59//
|p60  y/Am anva/icchad dhav/iSA vi/Sv/akarmAnt/ar arNav/e r/ajasi pr/aviSTAm /
     bhujiSy\a1M p/AtraM n/ihitaM g/uhA y/ad Av/ir bh/oge abhavan mAt.rm/adbhyaH //60//
|p61  tv/am asy Av/apanI j/anAnAm /aditiH kAmad/ughA paprathAn/A /
     y/at ta Un/aM t/at ta /A pUrayAti praj/ApatiH prathamaj/A .rt/asya //61//
|p62  upasth/As te anamIv/A ayakSm/A asm/abhyaM santu p.rthivi pr/asUtAH /

     saMvidAn/A div/A kave /Sriy/AM mA dhehi bh/UtyAm //63//
|c2
|p1  naD/am /A roha n/a te /atra lok/a id/aM s/IsaM bhAgadh/eyaM ta /ehi /
     y/o g/oSu y/akSmaH p/uruSeSu y/akSmas t/ena tv/aM sAk/am adhar/A.N p/arehi //1//
|p2  agha/SaMsaduH/SaMs/AbhyAM kar/eNAnukar/eNa ca /
     y/akSmaM ca s/arvaM t/enet/o m.rty/uM ca n/ir ajAmasi //2//
|p3  n/ir it/o m.rty/uM n/ir.rtiM n/ir /arAtim ajAmasi /
     y/o no dv/eSTi t/am addhy agne akravyAd y/am u dviSm/as t/am u te pr/a suvAmasi //3//
|p4  y/ady agn/iH kravy/Ad y/adi v/A vyAghr/a im/aM goSTh/aM praviv/e/S/AnyokAH /

|p5  y/at tvA kruddh/AH pracakr/ur many/unA p/uruSe m.rt/e /
     suk/alpam agne t/at tv/ayA p/unas tv/od dIpayAmasi //5//
|p6  p/unas tvAdity/A rudr/A v/asavaH p/unar brahm/A v/asunItir agne /
     p/unas tvA br/ahmaNas p/atir /AdhAd dIrghAyutv/Aya /Sat/a/SAradAya //6//

     t/aM harAmi pit.ryaj~N/Aya dUr/aM s/a gharm/am indhAM param/e sadh/asthe //7//
|p8  kravy/Adam agn/iM pr/a hiNomi dUr/am yam/arAj~No gacchatu ripravAh/aH /

|p13  asm/in vay/aM s/aMkasuke agna/u ripr/ANi m.rjmahe /
     /abhUma yaj~N/iyAH /Suddh/AH pr/a Na /AyUMSi tAriSat //13//
|p14  s/aMkasuko v/ikasuko nir.rth/o y/a/S ca nisvar/aH /
     t/e te y/akSmaM s/avedaso dUr/Ad dUr/am anIna/San //14//
|p15  y/o no /a/SveSu vIr/eSu y/o no g/oSv ajAv/iSu /
     kravy/AdaM n/ir nudAmasi y/o agn/ir janay/opanaH //15//
|p16  /anyebhyas tvA p/uruSebhyo g/obhyo /a/Svebhyas tvA /

|p17  y/asmin dev/A /am.rjata y/asmin manuSy\A ut/a /

|p18  s/amiddho agna Ahuta s/a no m/Abhy/apakramIH /

|p32  vy/Akaromi hav/iSAh/am eta/u ta/u br/ahmaNA vy \ah/aM kalpayAmi /

|p33  y/o no agn/iH pitaro h.rtsv \ant/ar Aviv/e/SAm/rto m/artyeSu /
     m/ayy ah/aM taM p/ari g.rhNAmi dev/aM m/A s/o asm/An dvikSata m/A vay/aM t/am //33//
|p34  apAv/rtya g/ArhapatyAt kravy/AdA pr/eta dakSiN/A /
     priy/aM pit/rbhya Atm/ane brahm/abhyaH k.rNutA priy/am //34//
|p35  dvibhAgadhan/am Ad/Aya pr/a kSiNAty /avartyA /
     agn/iH putr/asya jyeSTh/asya y/aH kravy/Ad /anirAhitah //35//
|p36  y/at k.rS/ate y/ad vanute y/ac ca vasn/ena vind/ate /
     s/arvaM m/artyasya t/an n/Asti kravy/Ac c/ed /anirAhitaH //36//
|p37  ayaj~Niy/o hat/avarcA bhavati na/inena hav/ir /attave /
     chin/atti k.rSy/A g/or dh/anAd y/aM kravy/Ad anuv/artate //37//
|p38  m/uhur g/rdhyaiH pr/a vadaty /Artim m/artyo n/Itya /
     kravy/Ad y/An agn/ir antik/Ad anuvidv/An vit/Avati //38//
|p39  gr/AhyA g.rh/AH s/aM s.rjyante striy/A y/an mriy/ate p/atiH /
     brahma/iv/a vidv/An eSy\o3 y/aH kravy/AdaM nirAd/adhat //39//
|p40  y/ad ripr/aM /S/amalaM cak.rm/a y/ac ca duSk.rt/am /
     /Apo mA t/asmAc chumbhantv agn/eH s/aMkasukAc ca y/at //40//

|p1  d/adAm/Ity ev/a brUyAd /anu cainAm /abhutsata /

|p16  c/ared ev/A traihAyaN/Ad /avij~NAtagadA sat/I /
     va/S/AM ca vidy/An nArada brAhmaN/As t/arhy eSy\AH //16//
|p17  y/a enAm /ava/SAm /Aha dev/AnAM n/ihitaM nidh/im /
     ubha/u t/asmai bhavA/Sarva/u parikr/amy/eSum asyatah //17//

     t/atra /Si/Sriye 'j/a /ekapAd/o 'd.rMhad dy/AvAp.rthiv/I b/alena //6//

     s/arvo ruroha r/ohito r/uhaH //26//
|p27  v/i mimISva p/ayasvatIM gh.rt/AcIM dev/AnAM dhen/ur /anapasp.rg eS/A /
     /indraH s/omaM pibatu kS/emo astv agn/iH pr/a stautu v/i m/rdho nudasva //27//

     abhIS/AT vi/SvAS/AD agn/iH sap/atnAn hantu y/e m/ama //28//

     y/at te sadh/asthaM param/e vy\oman //44//

|c2

|p1  y/a im/e dy/AvAp.rthiv/I jaj/Ana y/o dr/Apim k.rtv/A bh/uvanAni v/aste /

|p8  ahorAtra/ir v/imitaM triM/S/ada.NgaM trayoda/S/aM m/AsaM y/o nirm/imIte /

     t/a /Avav.rtran ts/adanAd .rt/asya /

|p10  y/at te candr/aM ka/Syapa rocan/Avad y/at saMhit/aM puSkal/aM citr/abhAnu y/asmin ts/UryA /ArpitAH sapt/a sAk/am /

     y/ad r/ohitam /ajanayanta dev/AH /

     /ud vepaya rohita pr/a kSiNIhi brahmajy/asya pr/ati mu~Nca p/A/SAn //12//

     tv/am im/A v/i/SvA bh/uvan/Anu tiSThasa .rt/asya p/anthAm /anv eSi vidv/AMs t/av/ed viSNo bahUdh/A vIry\ANi /
     tv/aM naH p.rNIhi pa/S/ubhir vi/Sv/arUpaiH sudh/AyAM mA dhehi param/e vy\oman //16//
|p17  pa~Nc/abhiH p/arA.N tapasy /ekayArv/A.N /a/Sastim eSi sud/ine b/AdhamAnas t/av/ed viSNo bahUdh/A vIry\ANi /
     tv/aM naH p.rNIhi pa/S/ubhir vi/Sv/arUpaiH sudh/AyAM mA dhehi param/e vy\oman //17//
|p18  tv/am /indras tv/am mahendr/as tv/aM lok/as tv/aM praj/ApatiH /
     t/ubhyaM yaj~N/o v/i tAyate t/ubhyaM juhvati j/uhvatas t/av/ed viSNo bahUdh/A vIry\ANi /
     tv/aM naH p.rNIhi pa/S/ubhir vi/Sv/arUpaiH sudh/AyAM mA dhehi param/e vy\oman //18//
|p19  /asati s/at pr/atiSThitaM sat/i bhUt/aM pr/atiSThitam /
     bhUt/am ha bh/avya /AhitaM bh/avyaM bhUt/e pr/atiSThitaM t/av/ed viSNo bahUdh/A vIry\ANi /
     tv/aM naH p.rNIhi pa/S/ubhir vi/Sv/arUpaiH sudh/AyAM mA dhehi param/e vy\oman //19//
|p20  /Sukr/o 'si bhrAj/o 'si /
     s/a y/athA tv/aM bhr/AjatA bhrAj/o 'sy ev/Ah/aM bhr/AjatA bhrAjyAsam //20//
|p21  r/ucir asi roc/o 'si /
     s/a y/athA tv/aM r/ucyA roc/o 'sy ev/Ah/aM pa/S/ubhi/S ca brAhmaNavarcas/ena ca ruciSIya //21//
|p22  udyat/e n/ama udAyat/e n/ama /uditAya n/amaH /
     vir/Aje n/amaH svar/Aje n/amaH samr/Aje n/amaH //22//
|p23  astaMyat/e n/amo 'stameSyat/e n/amo 'stamitAya n/amaH /
     vir/Aje n/amaH svar/Aje n/amah samr/Aje n/amaH //23//
|p24  /ud agAd ay/am Adity/o v/i/Svena t/apasA sah/a /
     sap/atnAn m/ahyaM randh/ayan m/A cAh/aM dviSat/e radhaM t/av/ed viSNo bahUdh/A vIry\ANi /
     tv/aM naH p.rNIhi pa/S/ubhir vi/Sv/arUpaiH sudh/AyAM mA dhehi param/e vy\oman //24//
|p25  /Aditya n/Avam /ArukSaH /Sat/AritrAM svast/aye /
     /ahar m/Aty apIparo r/AtriM satr/Ati pAraya //25//
|p26  sUrya nAvam ArukSaH /Sat/AritrAM svast/aye /
     r/AtriM m/Aty apIpar/o 'haH satr/Ati pAraya //26//
|p27  praj/Apater /Av.rto br/ahmaNA v/armaNAh/aM ka/Sy/apasya jy/otiSA v/arcasA ca /
     jar/adaSTiH k.rt/avIryo v/ihAyAH sah/asrAyuH s/uk.rta/S careyam //27//
|p28  p/ariv.rto br/ahmaNA v/armaNAh/am ka/Syapasya jy/otiSA v/arcasA ca /
     m/A mA pr/Apann /iSavo da/ivyA y/A m/A m/AnuSIr /avas.rSTAH vadh/Aya //28//
|p29  .rt/ena gupt/a .rt/ubhi/S ca s/arvair bhUt/ena gupt/o bh/avyena cAh/am /
     m/A mA pr/Apat pApm/A m/ot/a m.rty/ur ant/ar dadhe 'h/aM salil/ena vAc/aH //29//
|p30  agn/ir mA gopt/A p/ari pAtu vi/Sv/ataH udy/an ts/Uryo nudatAM m.rtyupA/S/An /
     vyucch/antIr uS/asaH p/arvatA dhruv/AH sah/asraM prAN/A m/ayy /A yatantAm //30//

|c1
|p1   /o cit s/akhAyaM sakhy/A vav.rtyAM tir/aH pur/u cid arNav/aM jaganv/An /

     /rSIn t/apasvato yama tapoj/A~M /api gacchatAt //15//

     y/e vA sah/asradakSiNAs t/AM cid ev/Api gacchatAt //17//

     ap/AM p/ayaso y/at p/ayas t/ena mA sah/a /Sumbhatu //56//

|p1  s/aMsaM sravantu nady\a1H s/aM v/AtAH s/aM patatr/iNaH /

|c2
|p1  /S/aM ta /Apo haimavat/IH /S/am u te santUtsy\AH /
     /S/aM te saniSyad/A /ApaH /S/am u te santu varSy\AH //1//
